The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
EXTRAORDINARY

PART IV (B) – LOCAL  GOVERNMENT
Local Government Notifications
wxl 2419$27 – 2025 ckjdß ui 17 jeks isl=rdod – 2025'01'17
No. 2419/27 – FRIDAY, JANUARY 17, 2025
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A – PG7000 – 05 (01/ 2025)
EHELIYAGODA PRADESHIYA SABHA
IT  is hereby published for the public to know that it has been decided under secretary decision no.  01 on. 03.10.2024 of 
no. 01 of the decision committee held on 03.10.2024 that the roads and lanes included in the schedule below should be 
declared as the roads and lanes owned by the Eheliyagoda Pradeshiya Sabha as the duty vested to the pradeshiya sabha 
of Sabaragamuwa province “the series of orders regarding the preparation of plans and publication of notices showing 
the list of roads and lanes maintain by the pradeshiya sabha of Sabaragamuwa Province” as publication by governor of 
Sabaragamuwa Province in the 
extraordinary gazette  no. 2316/20 dated 24th January 2023 to be read with section 24 of 
pradeshiya sabha act no. 15 of 1987.
 It is hereby announced that in order to prove their right to the said land, they should act before the expiry of a period of 
three month from the date of this announcement to file a case in the competent court, if it is the opinion of the party entitled 
to the land that any road or lane included in the said schedule passes through any land or part of any land.
 It is further announced that every road and lane included in the said schedule for which no such case has been assigned 
before the said period of three months shall be deemed to have been vested roads and lanes in the Eheliyagoda Pradeshiya 
Sabha.
  T.R.C.K. Gunasekara,
  Secretary and the implementation Officer
  Carrying out the functions
  Eheliyagoda Pradeshiya Sabha.
Eheliyagoda Pradeshiya Sabha,
15th January 2025.
